***tea.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tea.html>tea</a> (1648)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1"><a href = vnd.unilang:etymology.html>Etymology</a> 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:circa.html>Circa</a> 1650, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Min" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Min"><a href = vnd.unilang:min.html>Min</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nan.html>Nan</a></a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="nan">茶</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="nan-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tê</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Amoy_dialect" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Amoy dialect">Amoy <a href = vnd.unilang:dialect.html>dialect</a></a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Chinese" class="extiw" title="w:Old Chinese"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:chinese.html>Chinese</a></a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>ultimately</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sino-Tibetan_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Sino-Tibetan languages">Proto-Sino-Tibetan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sit-pro">*s-la</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:leaf.html>leaf</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:tea.html>tea</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
